# įå§įOllamaéåķå§éĢãĨæđīé§âŽ
from dotenv import load_dotenv
# åŊŪååæĩ ?envéåĶæŽĒéįšæĩéîîĻéæĐåšéåēîŦéĐæ §åĄįæĻšæđŠéĻå­åđæū§åĻå―éē?

# éūåģ°å―éîîĻéæĐåš
API = os.getenv('API')
OLLAMA_HOST = os.getenv('OLLAMA_HOST')
OLLAMA_MODEL = os.getenv('OLLAMA_MODEL')
DEEPSEEK_HOST = os.getenv('DEEPSEEK_HOST')
DEEPSEEK_MODEL = os.getenv('DEEPSEEK_MODEL')
DEEPSEEK_API_KEY = os.getenv('DEEPSEEK_API_KEY')
GEMINI_API_KEY = os.getenv('GEMINI_API_KEY')
GEMINI_MODEL = os.getenv('GEMINI_MODEL')
GEMINI_HOST = os.getenv('GEMINI_HOST')

ALLOWED_REFERENCE_EXTENSIONS = {"pdf", "txt", "md"}
MAX_REFERENCE_TEXT_CHARS = 20000

def parse_template_fields(template):
    """įï―į―åĶŊâæūæķî æŪįæĨî"""
    # æĩĢč·ĻæĪå§ï―åŊįãĻæŠåŊŪåŋå°Ūé°?{field_name} éįįīĄéĻåŦį§åĻ?
    pattern = r'\{([^}]+)\}'
    fields = re.findall(pattern, template)
    return list(set(fields))  # éåĐåļ

def load_prompt_template(field_name):
    """éįšæĩéŧæŪãįåķÄé?""
    prompt_file = os.path.join('prompts', f'{field_name}.txt')
    if not os.path.exists(prompt_file):
        raise FileNotFoundError(f'éŧæŪãįåķÄéæææĩ ?{prompt_file} æķåķįĻéĶ?)

    with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        return f.read()

def call_api(prompt):
    """éĒįļåéå­î"""
    # æĩ å·essionéūåģ°å―čĪ°æģåĒ æĩĢč·ĻæĪéĻåŽÄéĻåŽķįīæŋĄåįåĻâæđéæŽåĻéĒãĐįēŊįãæŪAPI
    current_api = session.get('selected_model', API)

    # éåŦįžåĻå äž
    messages = [
        {
            'role': 'system',
            'content': 'æĩĢįģæ§ļæķâŽæķîįŽæķæ°ąæŪéŅæđ°éæķįķéâåĒéåąūæŪéåŪåšéâįķé°å­įŽé åŦåĒ―éîæŪéåŠééå―æ―°é?
        },
        {
            'role': 'user',
            'content': prompt
        }
    ]
    # print(prompt)
    if current_api == 'deepseek':
        response = requests.post(
            DEEPSEEK_HOST,
            headers={
                'Authorization': f'Bearer {DEEPSEEK_API_KEY}',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json'
            },
            json={
                'model': DEEPSEEK_MODEL,
                'messages': messages,
                'temperature': 0.7,
                'max_tokens': 8192,
                'stream': False
            },
            timeout=300
        )
    elif current_api == 'gemini':
        response = requests.post(
            GEMINI_HOST,
            headers={
                'Authorization': f'Bearer {GEMINI_API_KEY}',
                'Content-Type': 'application/json'
            },
            json={
                'model': GEMINI_MODEL,
                'messages': messages,
                'temperature': 0.7,
                'stream': False
            },
            timeout=300
        )
    else:
        response = requests.post(
            OLLAMA_HOST,
            json={
                'model': OLLAMA_MODEL,
                'messages': messages,
                'stream': False
            }
        )

    if response.status_code != 200:
        if response.status_code == 402:
            raise Exception(f"DeepSeek API æĩĢæŽîæķåķåŧ")
        else:
            raise Exception(f"APIįåŠæĪæūķčūŦč§Ķ: {response.status_code} - {response.text}")

    # print("Response:", response.text)  # éĩæģåĩįđåąūæĢéåķį°ē

    try:
        response_data = response.json()

        if current_api == 'deepseek':
            if 'choices' in response_data and len(response_data['choices']) > 0:
                content = response_data['choices'][0]['message']['content'].strip()
            else:
                raise Exception("APIéåķį°ēéįįīĄéŋæŽîĪéæ°­æđ­éĩæ§åchoicesįæĨî")
        elif current_api == 'gemini':
            # éãæéîæé?zenmux.ai éĻ?APIéå åĻéĒã§čĒŦæĩž?DeepSeek éĻåŦæ·æīæįļåŊŪåŋĨįī
            if GEMINI_HOST and ('zenmux.ai' in GEMINI_HOST or 'api/v1' in GEMINI_HOST):
                # zenmux.ai éįįīĄéå ĒčĒŦæĩž?DeepSeeké?
                if 'choices' in response_data and len(response_data['choices']) > 0:
                    content = response_data['choices'][0]['message']['content'].strip()
                else:
                    raise Exception("APIéåķį°ēéįįīĄéŋæŽîĪéæ°­æđ­éĩæ§åchoicesįæĨî")
            else:
                # éå§åŊ Gemini éįįīĄ
                if 'candidates' in response_data and len(response_data['candidates']) > 0:
                    if 'content' in response_data['candidates'][0] and 'parts' in response_data['candidates'][0]['content']:
                        content = response_data['candidates'][0]['content']['parts'][0]['text'].strip()
                    else:
                        raise Exception("APIéåķį°ēéįįīĄéŋæŽîĪéæ°­æđ­éĩæ§åcontent.partsįæĨî")
                else:
                    raise Exception("APIéåķį°ēéįįīĄéŋæŽîĪéæ°­æđ­éĩæ§åcandidatesįæĨî")
        else:
            if 'message' in response_data and 'content' in response_data['message']:
                content = response_data['message']['content'].strip()
            else:
                raise Exception("APIéåķį°ēéįįīĄéŋæŽîĪéæ°­æđ­éĩæ§åmessage.contentįæĨî")

        # æĩĢč·ĻæĪå§ï―åŊįãĻæŠåŊŪåŋåđé?think>éåĐî·éåĐåūéå­î
        content = re.sub(r'<think>.*?</think>', '', content, flags=re.DOTALL)
        # print("Final content:", content)  # éĩæģåĩéâŽįžå åīįđ?
        return content.strip()
    except Exception as e:
        print("Error parsing response:", str(e))
        raise Exception(f"įï―į―APIéåķį°ēæūķčūŦč§Ķ: {str(e)}")

def get_characters(script_id, character_id=0):
    """éūåģ°å―įæåĢ"""
    if character_id == 0:
        characters = CharacterModel.query.filter_by(script_id=script_id).all()
    else:
        characters = CharacterModel.query.filter_by(script_id=script_id).filter(CharacterModel.id != character_id).all()

    if not characters:
        characters_json = "é?
    else:
        # įåîéđčķæĩéđî­čīįæĨåéæĨã
        characters_list = [
            {
                'name': character.name,
                'gender': character.gender,
                'age': character.age,
                'description': character.description,
                'personality': character.personality,
                'background': character.background,
                'relationships': character.relationships
            }
            for character in characters
        ]

        # įåîéđæåŠįãĻæĩéđî­čīJSONįæĨîæķ?
        characters_json = json.dumps(characters_list, ensure_ascii=False)

    return characters_json

def get_chapters(script_id, end_number=0):
    """éūåģ°å―æĩ å·nd_numberæķåŽŠåĒ éĻåŠį°ēįŧ?""
    if end_number == 0:
        chapters = ChapterModel.query.filter_by(script_id=script_id).order_by(ChapterModel.number.desc()).limit(5).all()
    else:
        chapters = ChapterModel.query.filter_by(script_id=script_id).filter(ChapterModel.number > end_number-5).limit(5).all()

    if not chapters:
        chapters_json = "é?
        from_number = 1
    else:
        # éļåĪį·éšåįīŠééåļæī?
        chapters = sorted(chapters, key=lambda chapter: chapter.number)

        # įåį·éšåæĩéđî­čīįæĨåéæĨã
        chapters_list = [
            {
                'number': chapter.number,
                'title': chapter.title,
                'chapter_outline': chapter.chapter_outline
            }
            for chapter in chapters
        ]

        # įåį·éšååŠįãĻæĩéđî­čīJSONįæĨîæķ?
        chapters_json = json.dumps(chapters_list, ensure_ascii=False)
        from_number = chapters[-1].number + 1
    return chapters_json, from_number

def get_one_chapter(script_id, number):
    """éūåģ°å―éļå§įūįŧįšåĶ­"""
    chapter = ChapterModel.query.filter_by(script_id=script_id).filter(ChapterModel.number == number).first()
    return chapter

@api.route('/validate', methods=['POST'])
@login_required
def validate():
    """æĨ åēįéĒįļåįéį°éĻåŦåžŽé?""
    data = request.get_json()
    field_name = data.get('field_name')
    optimize = data.get('optimize')

    try:
        # éįšæĩéŠč·šîĐéåå―įŧéļŋįåĶŊâæū
        prompt_template = load_prompt_template(field_name+optimize)

        # įï―į―åĶŊâæūæķî æŪįæĨî
        required_fields = parse_template_fields(prompt_template)
        if 'history' in required_fields:
            required_fields.remove('history')
        # åĶŦâŽéãĶæ§ļéïļ―åĒéåĪįđéâŽįæĨîéŪčåĄéŧæŠį·ĩæķæūįŽæķčđâ
        missing_fields = [field for field in required_fields if field not in data or not data[field]]

        if missing_fields:
            return jsonify({
                'success': False,
                'status': 'validation_failed',
                'message': f'įžåįŊčđå°îĶįæĨîéīæ §į§åĻåļčīįŧ? {", ".join(missing_fields)}'
            })

        # æĨ åēįéŦæ°ģįđéåēįđéĨįīåéįšå§ļéŽ?
        return jsonify({
            'success': True,
            'status': 'validation_passed',
            'message': 'æĨ åēįéŦæ°ģįđ'
        })

    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({
            'success': False,
            'status': 'validation_failed',
            'message': str(e)
        })

@api.route('/generate', methods=['POST'])
@login_required
def generate():
    """éĩŅîéå­îéĒįļå"""
    data = request.get_json()
    field_name = data.get('field_name')
    optimize = data.get('optimize')

    try:

        # éįšæĩéŠč·šîĐéåå―įŧéļŋįåĶŊâæū
        prompt_template = load_prompt_template(field_name+optimize)

        # éæåīēåĶŊâæūæķî æŪįæĨî
        prompt = build_prompt(field_name, data)

        # éĒįļåéå­î
        generated_content = call_api(prompt)

        return jsonify({
            'success': True,
            'status': 'generating_completed',
            'content': generated_content
        })

    except Exception as e:
        print(e)
        return jsonify({
            'success': False,
            'status': 'generating_failed',
            'message': str(e)
        })


@api.route('/generate/outline', methods=['POST'])
@login_required
def generate_outline():
    """éĒįļåæūķŅįŋ°"""
    data = request.get_json()
    script_id = data.get('script_id')
    field_name = data.get('field_name')
    optimize = data.get('optimize')

    try:
        # éįšæĩæūķŅįŋ°éĒįļåéŧæŪãįåķÄé?
        prompt_template = load_prompt_template(field_name+optimize)
        # æĩ åšĒæéđîžį°ąæķîĄåđéæ §įķéåķæ æĩåŽŽæŪéĩâŽéåĪîéđčŊ§įīéæåīēåĶŊâæūæķî æŪ{history}éŪãĨå
        data['history'] = get_characters(script_id)
        prompt = build_prompt(field_name, data)
        # éĒįļåéå­î
        generated_content = call_api(prompt)

        return jsonify({
            'success': True,
            'status': 'generating_completed',
            'content': generated_content
        })

    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({
            'success': False,
            'status': 'generating_failed',
            'message': str(e)
        })

@api.route('/generate/chapter', methods=['POST'])
@login_required
def generate_chapter():
    """éĒįļåéīæ Ķįī­éæ Ŧį·éšåæŪéåŊãéå­î"""
    data = request.get_json()
    script_id = int(data.get('script_id'))
    field_name = data.get('field_name')
    optimize = data.get('optimize')
    number = int(data.get('number'))

    try:
        # éįšæĩæūķŅįŋ°éĒįļåéŧæŪãįåķÄé?
        prompt_template = load_prompt_template(field_name+optimize)
        # æĩ åšĒæéđîžį°ąæķîĄåđéæ §įķéåķæ æĩåŽŽæŪéĩâŽéåĪîéđčŊ§įīéæåīēåĶŊâæūæķî æŪ{characters}éŪãĨå
        data['characters'] = get_characters(script_id)
        # æĩ åšĒæéđîžį°ąæķîĄåđéæ ĻæļķæĐæį°ēįŧįĩæŪæūķŅįŋ°éåąūæĩéđãĄÄéåĪļčéĻåhistory}éŪãĨå
        data['history'], _ = get_chapters(script_id, number-1)

        story = ScriptModel.query.filter_by(id=script_id).all()
        data['outline'] = story[0].outline
        data['background'] = story[0].background
        data['knowledge'] = story[0].knowledge
        data['write_style'] = story[0].write_style
        data['style'] = story[0].style
        # æĩ åšĒæéđîžį°ąæķîĄåđéæ ĻâŽæŋæ·ŪįĩįæĩéåąūæĩéđãĄÄéåĪļčéĻåmind_map}éŪãĨå
        mind_map = story[0].mind_map
        if mind_map == '' or mind_map == 'é?:
            mind_map = {}
        else:
            mind_map = json.loads(mind_map)
            for chapter in mind_map['data']['children']:
                if chapter['id'] == "chapter_"+str(number):
                    mind_map = chapter
                    break
        data['mind_map'] = json.dumps(mind_map, ensure_ascii=False)
        prompt = build_prompt(field_name, data)
        # éĒįļåéå­î
        generated_content = call_api(prompt)

        return jsonify({
            'success': True,
            'status': 'generating_completed',
            'content': generated_content
        })

    except Exception as e:
        print(e)
        return jsonify({
            'success': False,
            'status': 'generating_failed',
            'message': str(e)
        })

@api.route('/generate/mind', methods=['POST'])
@login_required
def generate_mind():
    """éĒįļåéŽæŋæ·Ūįĩįæĩ"""
    data = request.get_json()
    script_id = int(data.get('script_id'))
    title = data.get('title')
    field_name = data.get('field_name')

    try:
        # éįšæĩéŽæŋæ·ŪįĩįæĩéĒįļåéŧæŪãįåķÄé?
        prompt_template = load_prompt_template(field_name)
        number = 1
        mind_map = {'title':title, 'chapters':[]}
        while True:
            chapter = get_one_chapter(script_id, number)
            data['title'] = chapter.title
            data['number'] = chapter.number
            data['outline'] = chapter.chapter_outline
            prompt = build_prompt(field_name, data)
            generated_content = call_api(prompt)
            json_data = generated_content.replace('```json', '').replace('```', '')
            # įï―į―éĒįļåéĻå§SONéæŪįē
            mind_map['chapters'].append(json.loads(json_data))
            number += 1
        mind_map_json = json.dumps(mind_map, ensure_ascii=False)
        print(mind_map_json)
        return jsonify({
            'success': True,
            'status': 'generating_completed',
            'mind_map': mind_map_json
        })

    except Exception as e:
        print(e)
        return jsonify({
            'success': False,
            'status': 'generating_failed',
            'message': str(e)
        })

@api.route('/generate/chapters', methods=['POST'])
@login_required
def generate_chapters():
    """éĒįļåįŧįšåĶ­"""
    data = request.get_json()
    script_id = data.get('script_id')
    number = int(data.get('chapters_count'))
    try:
        # éįšæĩįŧįšåĶ­éĒįļåéŧæŪãįåķÄé?
        prompt_template = load_prompt_template('chapters')
        # æĩ åšĒæéđîžį°ąæķîĄåđéæ §įķéåķæ æĩåŽŽæŪéĩâŽéåĪîéđčŊ§įīéæåīēåĶŊâæūæķî æŪ{characters}éŪãĨå
        data['characters'] = get_characters(script_id)
        # æĩ åšĒæéđîžį°ąæķîĄåđéæ §įķéåķæ æĩåŽŽæŪéâŽæĐæį°ēįŧįįīéæåīēåĶŊâæūæķî æŪ{history}éŪãĨå
        chapters, from_number = get_chapters(script_id)
        data['history'] = chapters
        data['from'] = from_number
        data['to'] = from_number + number - 1
        # éæåīēéĩâŽéåĪį§åĻ?
        prompt = build_prompt(field_name, data)
        # éĒįļåéå­î
        generated_content = call_api(prompt)
        json_data = generated_content.replace('```json', '').replace('```', '')
        # įï―į―éĒįļåéĻå§SONéæŪįē
        chapters = json.loads(json_data)
        # æ·æŋįĻįæåĢéįæéđîžį°ą
        for chapter_data in chapters:
            chapter = ChapterModel(
                script_id=int(script_id),
                number=int(chapter_data.get('number')),
                title=str(chapter_data.get('title')),
                chapter_outline=str(chapter_data.get('outline')),
                chapter_content='',
                chapter_script=''
            )
            db.session.add(chapter)

        # éŧæŠæ°ĶæĩåŽŠå§
        db.session.commit()

        return jsonify({
            'success': True,
            'status': 'generating_completed',
            'message': f'éīæŽå§éĒįļå {len(chapters)} æķîį·éš?
        })

    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return jsonify({
            'success': False,
            'status': 'generating_failed',
            'message': 'éĒįļåéĻåŦåīįđéįŽéîæđéå ĒæŪJSONéįįīĄ'
        })
    except Exception as e:
        # éæ æéŋæŽîĪéč·šæīåĐæ°Ŧį°Ļé?
        db.session.rollback()
        print(e)
        return jsonify({
            'success': False,
            'status': 'generating_failed',
            'message': str(e)
        })

@api.route('/generate/characters', methods=['POST'])
@login_required
def generate_characters():
    """éĒįļåįæåĢ"""
    data = request.get_json()
    script_id = data.get('script_id')

    try:
        # éįšæĩįæåĢéĒįļåéŧæŪãįåķÄé?
        prompt_template = load_prompt_template('characters')
        # æĩ åšĒæéđîžį°ąæķîĄåđéæ §įķéåķæ æĩåŽŽæŪéĩâŽéåĪîéđ?
        # éæåīēåĶŊâæūæķî æŪ{history}éŪãĨå

        # éĒįļåéå­î

        json_data = generated_content.replace('```json', '').replace('```', '')
        # įï―į―éĒįļåéĻå§SONéæŪįē
        characters = json.loads(json_data)
        # æ·æŋįĻįæåĢéįæéđîžį°ą
        for character_data in characters:
            character = CharacterModel(
                script_id=script_id,
                name=character_data.get('name', ''),
                gender=character_data.get('gender', 'éæĩįēŽ'),
                age=character_data.get('age'),
                description=character_data.get('description', ''),
                personality=character_data.get('personality', ''),
                background=character_data.get('background', ''),
                relationships=character_data.get('relationships', '')
            )
            db.session.add(character)

        # éŧæŠæ°ĶæĩåŽŠå§
        db.session.commit()

        return jsonify({
            'success': True,
            'status': 'generating_completed',
            'message': f'éīæŽå§éĒįļå {len(characters)} æķîîéđ?
        })

    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return jsonify({
            'success': False,
            'status': 'generating_failed',
            'message': 'éĒįļåéĻåŦåīįđéįŽéîæđéå ĒæŪJSONéįįīĄ'

@api.route('/optimize/character', methods=['POST'])
@login_required
def optimize_character():
    """æĩžæĻšåŊēįæåĢ"""
    data = request.get_json()
    script_id = data.get('script_id')
    character_id = data.get('character_id')

    try:
        # éįšæĩįæåĢæĩžæĻšåŊēéŧæŪãįåķÄé?
        prompt_template = load_prompt_template('character_optimize')
        # æĩ åšĒæéđîžį°ąæķîĄåđéæ ­æŦæĩåįķéåķîéđčđ­įŪĢæūķæ ŦæŪéæĩįēŽįæåĢéåąūæĩéđãĄÄéåĪļčéĻåhistory}éŪãĨå
        data['history'] = get_characters(script_id, character_id)
        prompt = build_prompt(field_name, data)
        # éĒįļåéå­î
        generated_content = call_api(prompt)

        json_data = generated_content.replace('```json', '').replace('```', '')
        # įï―į―éĒįļåéĻå§SONéæŪįē
        character_data = json.loads(json_data)
        # æ·æŋįĻįæåĢéįæéđîžį°ą
        character = CharacterModel.query.filter_by(id=character_id).first()
        character.description = character_data.get('description')
        character.personality = character_data.get('personality')
        character.background = character_data.get('background')
        character.relationships = character_data.get('relationships')
        # éĐå­åļīéŧæŠæ°Ķéå­æžéåąžįŽéâŽįä――įéĒâąpdate
        db.session.commit()

        return jsonify({
            'success': True,
            'status': 'generating_completed',
            'message': 'éīæŽå§æĩžæĻšåŊēįæåĢ',
            'description': character.description,
            'personality': character.personality,
            'background': character.background,
            'relationships': character.relationships
        })

    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return jsonify({
            'success': False,
            'status': 'generating_failed',
            'message': 'éĒįļåéĻåŦåīįđéįŽéîæđéå ĒæŪJSONéįįīĄ'
        })
    except Exception as e:
        # éæ æéŋæŽîĪéč·šæīåĐæ°Ŧį°Ļé?
        db.session.rollback()
        return jsonify({
            'success': False,
            'status': 'generating_failed',
            'message': str(e)
        })


@api.route('/validate_content', methods=['GET'])
@login_required
def validate_content():
    """æĨ åēįéåŽį°Ļéå­îéīæ §åĒ―éîåīįđ?""
    try:
        script_id = request.args.get('script_id', type=int)
        content_type = request.args.get('type', 'story')  # 'story' éī?'script'

        if not script_id:
            return jsonify({
                'success': False,
                'message': 'įžåįŊscript_idéåæ'
            }), 400

        # éūåģ°å―éŅæđ°
        script = ScriptModel.query.get_or_404(script_id)
        if script.user_id != current_user.id:
            return jsonify({
                'success': False,
                'message': 'éŪãĶįéåĪæ―éæ°įįä―đîéŅæđ°'
            }), 403

        # éč§åĩįŧŦčŊēį·éūåģ°å―éå­î
        if content_type == 'story':
            # éūåģ°å―éĩâŽéåĪį·éšåæŪéåŽį°Ļéå­î
            chapters = ChapterModel.query.filter_by(script_id=script_id).order_by(ChapterModel.number).all()
            content = f"éåĶ script.title}éåŠn\n"
            for chapter in chapters:
                content += f"\nįŧįchapter.number}įŧ?{chapter.title}\n\n"
                if hasattr(chapter, 'chapter_content') and chapter.chapter_content:
                    content += chapter.chapter_content + "\n"
                else:
                    content += getattr(chapter, 'content', '(įŧįšåĶ­éå­îæķčđâ)') + "\n"
        elif content_type == 'script':
            # éūåģ°å―éĩâŽéåĪį·éšåæŪéŅæđ°éå­î
            chapters = ChapterModel.query.filter_by(script_id=script_id).order_by(ChapterModel.number).all()
            characters = CharacterModel.query.filter_by(script_id=script_id).all()
            content = f"éåĶ script.title}éåŽŠåĒ―éįn\n"
            if characters:
                content += "éæŊîéđčķãéæ­n\n"
                for character in characters:
                    content += f"{character.name}: {character.gender}, {character.age}åŪäđn"
                    if character.description:
                        content += f"éŧåŋå Š: {character.description}\n"
                    content += "\n"
            for chapter in chapters:
                content += f"\nįŧįchapter.number}įŧ?{chapter.title}\n\n"
                if hasattr(chapter, 'chapter_script') and chapter.chapter_script:
                    content += chapter.chapter_script + "\n"
                else:
                    content += "(įŧįšåĶ­éŅæđ°éå­îæķčđâ)\n"
        else:
            return jsonify({
                'success': False,
                'message': 'æķåķæŪéļä―šæŪéå­îįŧŦčŊēį·'
            }), 400

        # éįšæĩæĨ åēįéŧæŪãįåķÄé?
        try:
            prompt_template = load_prompt_template('content_check')
        except FileNotFoundError:
            return jsonify({
                'success': False,
                'message': 'æĨ åēįéŧæŪãįåķÄéæææĩ æĩįŽįæĻšæđŠ'
            }), 500

        # éåŦįžįđåąūæĢéĻåŽå―įŧéļŋį
        prompt = f"{prompt_template}\n\néæ­į°ŪéåĻæđ°éæ­n\n{content}"

        # įåŠæĪAIæĐæķîæĨ åēį
        validation_result = call_api(prompt)

        return jsonify({
            'success': True,
            'validation_result': validation_result,
            'message': 'æĨ åēįįđåąūå'
        })

    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({
            'success': False,
            'message': f'æĨ åēįæūķčūŦč§Ķ: {str(e)}'
        }), 500

# =========================
# Chat MVP APIéå Ģæ·éįēå api.py éåĶæŽĒéîĒįŽé?
# =========================
# æĩ čŊēå§éå­įĻįæĻšåéåĄVP éå Žįī
# åĻãĶå°éæ°ģįđéîåīįæĻšįĻéîįīéåķå§éēåķæéåšįī°æķã ã
DEFAULT_WORD_COUNT = "2"
CHAT_TASK_STORE = {}
CHAT_TASK_LOCK = threading.Lock()


def _set_chat_task(task_id, **kwargs):
    """įŧūč·ĻâžįđåĪåéĶįæīŋééĒæĒéïžå§ļéŽ?""
    with CHAT_TASK_LOCK:
        task = CHAT_TASK_STORE.get(task_id, {})
        task["task_id"] = task_id
        task.update(kwargs)
        CHAT_TASK_STORE[task_id] = task


def _get_chat_task(task_id):
    """įŧūč·ĻâžįđåĪåéĶæî°éæ ĶæĒéïžå§ļéŽ?""
    with CHAT_TASK_LOCK:
        return CHAT_TASK_STORE.get(task_id)


def _normalize_tag_list(value):
    """éķåĐį§įŧïļŋčĶ / éæĨãįžįķįŦīæîåéåĐåļéåšĢæŪįæĨîæķæåŠį?""
    if value is None:
        return []

    if isinstance(value, list):
        raw = value
    elif isinstance(value, str):
        raw = re.split(r"[é?é?|é?]+", value)
    else:
        raw = [str(value)]

    result = []
    seen = set()
    for item in raw:
        text = str(item).strip()
        if not text:
            continue
        if text not in seen:
            seen.add(text)
            result.append(text)
    return result


def _normalize_word_count_wan(value):
    try:
        v = float(value)
        if v <= 0:
            return DEFAULT_WORD_COUNT
        return v
    except Exception:
        return DEFAULT_WORD_COUNT

@api.route('/project/<int:project_id>/trace', methods=['GET'])
@login_required
def get_project_trace(project_id):
    """
    éūåģ°å―æĐåĐâžé―æĻŋîĶ
    """
    script = ScriptModel.query.get_or_404(project_id)
    if script.user_id != current_user.id:
        return jsonify({
            'success': False,
            'message': 'éŪãĶįéåĪæ―éæŊîéîŋîæĪĪå­æī°'
        }), 403

    latest_trace = []
    latest_task_id = None
    latest_status = None

    with CHAT_TASK_LOCK:
        for task_id, task in CHAT_TASK_STORE.items():
            if task.get('project_id') == project_id:
                latest_trace = task.get('trace', [])
                latest_task_id = task_id
                latest_status = task.get('status')

    return jsonify({
        'success': True,
        'project_id': project_id,
        'task_id': latest_task_id,
        'status': latest_status,
        'trace': latest_trace
    })
